resolve chapter of manga 

curl -X 'GET' \
  'http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/mangas/resolve_chapter?upload_url=https%3A%2F%2Fzonatmo.com%2Fview_uploads%2F1644409&force_refresh=false' \
  -H 'accept: application/json'

  {
  "final_url": "https://zonatmo.com/viewer/ad7c72e01ddf80e081fe15fa854559ea/paginated"
}

Manga filtros estáticos

  'http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/mangas/filters' \
  -H 'accept: application/json'

  {
  "filters": {
    "title": {
